    65	async function fetchYahooSeries(symbol: string): Promise<TrustedSeriesPoint & { change5d: number | null }> {
    66	  const url = `https://query2.finance.yahoo.com/v8/finance/chart/${encodeURIComponent(
    67	    symbol,
    68	  )}?interval=1d&range=1mo`;
    69	  const payload = await fetchJson<YahooChartResponse>(url);
    70	  const result = payload?.chart?.result?.[0];
    71	  const timestamps = result?.timestamp ?? [];
    72	  const closes = result?.indicators?.quote?.[0]?.close ?? [];
    73	
    74	  let latestClose: number | null = null;
    75	  let latestTs: number | null = null;
    76	  for (let i = closes.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
    77	    const close = closes[i];
    78	    if (typeof close === "number" && Number.isFinite(close)) {
    79	      latestClose = close;
    80	      latestTs = timestamps[i] ?? null;
    81	      break;
    82	    }
    83	  }
    84	
    85	  let anchorClose: number | null = null;
    86	  let validSeen = 0;
    87	  for (let i = closes.length - 1; i >= 0; i -= 1) {
    88	    const close = closes[i];
    89	    if (typeof close !== "number" || !Number.isFinite(close)) continue;
    90	    validSeen += 1;
    91	    if (validSeen >= 6) {
    92	      anchorClose = close;
    93	      break;
    94	    }
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  const change5d =
    98	    latestClose !== null && anchorClose !== null && anchorClose !== 0
    99	      ? (latestClose - anchorClose) / anchorClose
   100	      : null;
   101	
   102	  return {
   103	    value: latestClose,
   104	    asOf: toDateIso(latestTs ?? result?.meta?.regularMarketTime ?? null),
   105	    source: "Yahoo Finance",
   106	    url,
   107	    change5d,
   108	  };
   109	}
   110	
   111	async function fetchFredLatest(seriesId: string): Promise<TrustedSeriesPoint> {
   112	  const url = `https://fred.stlouisfed.org/graph/fredgraph.csv?id=${encodeURIComponent(seriesId)}`;
   113	  try {
   114	    const res = await fetch(url, { cache: "no-store" });
   115	    if (!res.ok) {
   116	      return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   117	    }
   118	    const csv = await res.text();
   119	    const lines = csv.trim().split("\n");
   120	    for (let i = lines.length - 1; i >= 1; i -= 1) {
   121	      const row = lines[i];
   122	      const [date, value] = row.split(",", 2);
   123	      if (!date || !value || value === ".") continue;
   124	      const n = Number(value);
   125	      if (!Number.isFinite(n)) continue;
   126	      return {
   127	        value: n,
   128	        asOf: new Date(`${date}T00:00:00Z`).toISOString(),
   129	        source: "FRED",
   130	        url,
   131	      };
   132	    }
   133	  } catch {
   134	    return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   135	  }
   136	  return { value: null, asOf: null, source: "FRED", url };
   137	}

   139	export async function fetchTrustedMarketSnapshot(): Promise<TrustedMarketSnapshot> {
   140	  const [zl, cl, cny, vix, ovx] = await Promise.all([
   141	    fetchYahooSeries("ZL=F"),
   142	    fetchYahooSeries("CL=F"),
   143	    fetchYahooSeries("CNY=X"),
   144	    fetchFredLatest("VIXCLS"),
   145	    fetchFredLatest("OVXCLS"),
   146	  ]);
   147	
   148	  return {
   149	    fetchedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
   150	    zl,
   151	    cl,
   152	    cny,
   153	    vix,
   154	    ovx,
   155	  };
   156	}

   160	    .filter((u, idx, arr) => typeof u === "string" && arr.indexOf(u) === idx);

    23	  - App Router

    25	  - Proxy

    47	
    48	The above will also clone the Starter kit to your GitHub, you can clone that locally and develop locally.
    49	
    50	If you wish to just develop locally and not deploy to Vercel, [follow the steps below](#clone-and-run-locally).
    51	
    52	## Clone and run locally
    53	
    54	1. You'll first need a Supabase project which can be made [via the Supabase dashboard](https://database.new)
    55	
    56	2. Create a Next.js app using the Supabase Starter template npx command
    57	
    58	   ```bash
    59	   npx create-next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    60	   ```
    61	
    62	   ```bash
    63	   yarn create next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    64	   ```
    65	
    66	   ```bash
    67	   pnpm create next-app --example with-supabase with-supabase-app
    68	   ```
    69	
    70	3. Use `cd` to change into the app's directory
    71	
    72	   ```bash
    73	   cd with-supabase-app
    74	   ```
    75	
    76	4. Rename `.env.example` to `.env.local` and update the following:
    77	
    78	  ```env
    79	  NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL=[INSERT SUPABASE PROJECT URL]
    80	  NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY=[INSERT SUPABASE PROJECT API PUBLISHABLE OR ANON KEY]
    81	  ```
    82	  > [!NOTE]
    83	  > This example uses `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY`, which refers to Supabase's new **publishable** key format.
    84	  > Both legacy **anon** keys and new **publishable** keys can be used with this variable name during the transition period. Supabase's dashboard may show `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_ANON_KEY`; its value can be used in this example.
    85	  > See the [full announcement](https://github.com/orgs/supabase/discussions/29260) for more information.
    86	
    87	  Both `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_URL` and `NEXT_PUBLIC_SUPABASE_PUBLISHABLE_KEY` can be found in [your Supabase project's API settings](https://supabase.com/dashboard/project/_?showConnect=true)
    88	
    89	5. You can now run the Next.js local development server:
    90	
    91	   ```bash
    92	   npm run dev
    93	   ```
    94	
    95	   The starter kit should now be running on [localhost:3000](http://localhost:3000/).
    96	
    97	6. This template comes with the default shadcn/ui style initialized. If you instead want other ui.shadcn styles, delete `components.json` and [re-install shadcn/ui](https://ui.shadcn.com/docs/installation/next)
    98	
    99	> Check out [the docs for Local Development](https://supabase.com/docs/guides/getting-started/local-development) to also run Supabase locally.
   100

    65	### Process Rules
    66	
    67	1. **Read the migration plan before touching code.** It defines every table, route, job, and phase.
    68	2. **Follow the phase order.** Phase 0 before Phase 1. Phase 1 before Phase 2. No skipping.
    69	3. **Run evaluation gates.** Each phase has specific checks. Don't declare done until they pass.
    70	4. **One task at a time.** Finish what was asked before touching anything else.
    71	5. **No "while I'm here" refactors.** Stay scoped.
    72	6. **Memory first.** Search memory at session start, store decisions immediately.
    73	7. **Brainstorm before building.** Use the superpowers brainstorming skill for any non-trivial feature.
    74	8. **Verify before claiming done.** Use the superpowers verification skill.
    75	9. **Checkpoint before implementation.** For non-trivial planning work, audit repo reality first, structure the plan as numbered decision checkpoints, run one Ralph Loop per checkpoint, and update docs after each locked decision.
    76	10. **Fail-closed completion.** Read `docs/INDEX.md`, `docs/MASTER_PLAN.md`, and `docs/agent-safety-gates.md` at startup. If any required check is `FAIL`, `NOT RUN`, warning-only, or aborted, report `STATUS: INCOMPLETE`.
    77	11. **Source and generated artifacts are separate lanes.** Source/config/tooling changes require generated `quality/` artifacts to be regenerated and verified before quality can be claimed current.
    78	12. **Docs/contracts update in the same change.** Any behavior, config, schema, gate, or operational-truth change must update the relevant docs/contracts in the same change.

    46	  return dateStr.slice(0, 10) as unknown as Time;
    47	}
    48	
    49	function computeVolatility(bars: ZlPriceBar[]): string {
    50	  const recent = bars.slice(-20);
    51	  if (recent.length < 2) return "--";
    52	  const returns: number[] = [];
    53	  for (let i = 1; i < recent.length; i++) {
    54	    returns.push(Math.log(recent[i].close / recent[i - 1].close));
    55	  }
    56	  const mean = returns.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / returns.length;
    57	  const variance =
    58	    returns.reduce((a, b) => a + (b - mean) ** 2, 0) / returns.length;
    59	  return (Math.sqrt(variance) * Math.sqrt(252) * 100).toFixed(1) + "%";
    60	}
    61	
    62	function computeSmaData(candles: CandlestickData<Time>[], period: number): { time: Time; value: number }[] {
    63	  if (candles.length < period) return [];
    64	
    65	  const result: { time: Time; value: number }[] = [];
    66	  let rollingSum = 0;
    67	
    68	  for (let i = 0; i < candles.length; i += 1) {
    69	    rollingSum += candles[i].close;
    70	    if (i >= period) {
    71	      rollingSum -= candles[i - period].close;
    72	    }
    73	    if (i >= period - 1) {
    74	      result.push({
    75	        time: candles[i].time,
    76	        value: rollingSum / period,
    77	      });
    78	    }
    79	  }
    80	
    81	  return result;
    82	}

   106	    async function fetchBars() {

   108	        const res = await fetch("/api/zl/price-1d", { cache: "no-store" });
   109	        if (!res.ok) return;

   125	        setBars(parsed);
   126	
   127	        const latest = parsed[parsed.length - 1];
   128	        const prev = parsed[parsed.length - 2];
   129	        setLastPrice(latest.close);
   130	        setHighPrice(latest.high);
   131	        setLowPrice(latest.low);
   132	        setVolatility(computeVolatility(parsed));
   133	
   134	        if (prev) {
   135	          setPriceChange(((latest.close - prev.close) / prev.close) * 100);
   136	        }
   137	      } catch {
   138	        /* fail silently — chart stays empty */
   139	      }
   140	    }
   141	
   142	    fetchBars();
   143	    const id = setInterval(fetchBars, REFRESH_MS);
   144	    return () => clearInterval(id);
   145	  }, []);
   146	
   147	  // Create and manage chart
   148	  useEffect(() => {
   149	    if (!containerRef.current || bars.length === 0) return;
   150	
   151	    // Clean up previous
   152	    if (chartRef.current) {
   153	      try {
   154	        chartRef.current.remove();
   155	      } catch {
   156	        /* already disposed */
   157	      }
   158	      chartRef.current = null;
   159	      seriesRef.current = null;
   160	      fitCalledRef.current = false;
   161	    }
   162	
   163	    const chart = createChart(containerRef.current, {
   164	      layout: {
   165	        background: { type: ColorType.Solid, color: "transparent" },
   166	        textColor: TEXT_COLOR,
   167	        fontFamily: "Inter, sans-serif",
   168	        fontSize: 11,
   169	        attributionLogo: false,
   170	      },
   171	      grid: {
   172	        vertLines: { color: GRID_COLOR },
   173	        horzLines: { color: GRID_COLOR },
   174	      },
   175	      crosshair: {
   176	        vertLine: {
   177	          color: CROSSHAIR_COLOR,
   178	          width: 1,
   179	          style: LineStyle.Solid,
   180	          labelBackgroundColor: LABEL_BG,
   181	        },
   182	        horzLine: {
   183	          color: CROSSHAIR_COLOR,
   184	          width: 1,
   185	          style: LineStyle.Solid,
   186	          labelBackgroundColor: LABEL_BG,
   187	        },
   188	      },
   189	      rightPriceScale: {
   190	        borderColor: "transparent",
   191	        autoScale: true,
   192	        scaleMargins: { top: 0.05, bottom: 0.05 },
   193	      },
   194	      timeScale: {
   195	        borderColor: "transparent",
   196	        timeVisible: false,
   197	        fixLeftEdge: false,
   198	        fixRightEdge: false,
   199	        rightOffset: RIGHT_PADDING_BARS,
   200	        barSpacing: BAR_SPACING,
   201	        minBarSpacing: MIN_BAR_SPACING,
   202	        lockVisibleTimeRangeOnResize: true,
   203	      },
   204	      handleScroll: {
   205	        mouseWheel: false,
   206	        pressedMouseMove: true,
   207	        horzTouchDrag: true,
   208	        vertTouchDrag: false,
   209	      },
   210	      handleScale: {
   211	        mouseWheel: false,
   212	        pinch: true,
   213	        axisPressedMouseMove: { time: true, price: true },
   214	        axisDoubleClickReset: { time: true, price: true },
   215	      },
   216	    });
   217	
   218	    chartRef.current = chart;
   219	
   220	    // Build candlestick data sorted chronologically
   221	    const candleData: CandlestickData<Time>[] = bars
   222	      .map((b) => ({
   223	        time: toChartDay(b.tradeDate),
   224	        open: b.open,
   225	        high: b.high,
   226	        low: b.low,
   227	        close: b.close,
   228	      }))
   229	      .sort((a, b) => String(a.time).localeCompare(String(b.time)));
   230	
   231	    const series = chart.addSeries(CandlestickSeries, {
   232	      upColor: CANDLE_THEME.upColor,
   233	      downColor: CANDLE_THEME.downColor,
   234	      borderUpColor: CANDLE_THEME.borderUpColor,
   235	      borderDownColor: CANDLE_THEME.borderDownColor,
   236	      wickUpColor: CANDLE_THEME.wickUpColor,
   237	      wickDownColor: CANDLE_THEME.wickDownColor,
   238	      priceLineVisible: true,
   239	    });
   240	
   241	    series.setData(candleData);
   242	    seriesRef.current = series;
   243	
   244	    const smaData = computeSmaData(candleData, SMA_PERIOD);
   245	    if (smaData.length > 0) {
   246	      const smaSeries = chart.addSeries(LineSeries, {
   247	        color: SMA_COLOR,
   248	        lineWidth: SMA_WIDTH,
   249	        lineStyle: LineStyle.Solid,
   250	        priceLineVisible: false,
   251	        lastValueVisible: false,
   252	        crosshairMarkerVisible: false,
   253	      });
   254	      smaSeries.setData(smaData);
   255	    }
   256	
   257	    const pivotPrimitive = new PivotLinesPrimitive();
   258	    const forecastTargetsPrimitive = new ForecastTargetsPrimitive();
   259	    series.attachPrimitive(pivotPrimitive);
   260	    if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {
   261	      series.attachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);
   262	    }
   263	
   264	    // Forecast target zones should be projected near the most recent bars, not full-width.
   265	    if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {
   266	      const targetStartIndex = Math.max(0, candleData.length - 16);
   267	      const targetStartTime = candleData[targetStartIndex]?.time;
   268	      forecastTargetsPrimitive.setTargetZones(targetZones, targetStartTime);
   269	    }
   270	
   271	    // Fib rendering: anchored start, pivot zone fill, and structural-break lock.
   272	    const fibCandles: CandleData[] = bars.map((b, idx) => ({
   273	      time: idx,
   274	      open: b.open,
   275	      high: b.high,
   276	      low: b.low,
   277	      close: b.close,
   278	      volume: b.volume,
   279	    }));
   280	
   281	    const currentPrice = bars[bars.length - 1]?.close;
   282	    let fibResult = fibLockedRef.current;
   283	    if (
   284	      !fibResult ||
   285	      currentPrice == null ||
   286	      currentPrice > fibResult.anchorHigh ||
   287	      currentPrice < fibResult.anchorLow
   288	    ) {
   289	      fibResult = calculateFibonacciMultiPeriod(fibCandles);
   290	      fibLockedRef.current = fibResult;
   291	    }
   292	
   293	    if (fibResult) {
   294	      const anchorIdx = Math.min(
   295	        fibResult.anchorHighBarIndex,
   296	        fibResult.anchorLowBarIndex,
   297	      );
   298	      const anchorStartTime = candleData[anchorIdx]?.time;
   299	      pivotPrimitive.setFibResult(fibResult, anchorStartTime);
   300	    } else {
   301	      pivotPrimitive.setFibResult(null);
   302	    }
   303	
   304	    // Set initial visible range: last N bars + right padding
   305	    if (!fitCalledRef.current && candleData.length > 0) {
   306	      const total = candleData.length;
   307	      const visible = Math.min(INITIAL_VISIBLE_BARS, total);
   308	      chart.timeScale().setVisibleLogicalRange({
   309	        from: Math.max(0, total - visible),
   310	        to: total - 1 + RIGHT_PADDING_BARS,
   311	      });
   312	      fitCalledRef.current = true;
   313	    }
   314	
   315	    // Responsive resize
   316	    let disposed = false;
   317	    const observer = new ResizeObserver((entries) => {
   318	      if (disposed || !entries[0]) return;
   319	      const { width, height: h } = entries[0].contentRect;
   320	      try {
   321	        chart.applyOptions({ width, height: h });
   322	      } catch {
   323	        /* disposed */
   324	      }
   325	    });
   326	    observer.observe(containerRef.current);
   327	
   328	    return () => {
   329	      disposed = true;
   330	      observer.disconnect();
   331	      try {
   332	        if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {
   333	          series.detachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);
   334	        }
   335	        series.detachPrimitive(pivotPrimitive);
   336	        chart.remove();
   337	      } catch {
   338	        /* disposed */
   339	      }
   340	    };
   341	  }, [bars, targetZones]);
   342	
   343	  const changeColor = priceChange >= 0 ? "#26C6DA" : "#EC0000";
   344	
   345	  return (
   346	    <div
   347	      className="relative w-full rounded-xl overflow-hidden border border-white/5 flex flex-col"
   348	      style={{
   349	        background: "linear-gradient(180deg, #131722 0%, #0d1117 100%)",
   350	        height: typeof height === "number" ? `${height}px` : height,
   351	      }}
   352	    >
   353	      {/* Header */}
   354	      <div className="flex-shrink-0 flex items-center justify-between px-4 py-2 border-b border-white/5">
   355	        <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
   356	          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   357	            <div className="w-2 h-2 rounded-full bg-cyan-400 shadow-lg shadow-cyan-400/50" />
   358	            <span className="text-sm font-semibold text-white tracking-tight">
   359	              ZL1!
   360	            </span>
   361	          </div>
   362	          <span className="text-[11px] text-white/30 font-medium">
   363	            Soybean Oil &bull; 1D
   364	          </span>
   365	        </div>
   366	        <div className="flex items-center gap-4">
   367	          {highPrice != null && lowPrice != null && (
   368	            <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-[11px]">
   369	              <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
   370	                <span className="text-white/30">H</span>
   371	                <span className="text-white/60 font-mono">
   372	                  {highPrice.toFixed(2)}
   373	                </span>
   374	              </div>
   375	              <div className="flex items-center gap-1">
   376	                <span className="text-white/30">L</span>
   377	                <span className="text-white/60 font-mono">
   378	                  {lowPrice.toFixed(2)}
   379	                </span>
   380	              </div>
   381	            </div>
   382	          )}
   383	          <div className="h-3 w-px bg-white/10" />
   384	          <div className="flex items-center gap-1 px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded bg-white/5">
   385	            <span className="text-[9px] text-white/30 uppercase">IV</span>
   386	            <span className="text-[11px] font-mono text-cyan-400">
   387	              {volatility}
   388	            </span>
   389	          </div>
   390	          {lastPrice != null && (
   391	            <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
   392	              <span className="text-xl font-semibold text-white tabular-nums">
   393	                {lastPrice.toFixed(2)}
   394	              </span>
   395	              <span
   396	                className="text-xs font-medium tabular-nums"
   397	                style={{ color: changeColor }}
   398	              >
   399	                {priceChange >= 0 ? "+" : ""}
   400	                {priceChange.toFixed(2)}%
   401	              </span>
   402	            </div>
   403	          )}
   404	        </div>
   405	      </div>
   406	
   407	      {/* Chart area */}
   408	      <div className="relative w-full flex-1 min-h-0">
   409	        {/* Watermark overlay */}
   410	        <div className="absolute inset-0 flex items-center justify-center pointer-events-none z-[1]">

    49	        helper = read_text("lib/server/ingest-run.ts")
    50	        sql_intraday = read_text("supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql")

    55	        self.assertTrue(helper_statuses, "Expected TS helper status literals to be present.")
    56	        self.assertTrue(sql_statuses, "Expected SQL status literals to be present.")
    57

   214	class BoundaryAndEdgeCaseTests(unittest.TestCase):

   216	        """[Req: inferred — from mkt schema tables] both intraday table levels exist."""

   221	    def test_boundary_horizon_allowlist_parity_across_routes(self) -> None:
   222	        """[Req: inferred — REQ-002 parity pattern] horizon allowlist should match across forecast routes."""
   223	        forecast = read_text("app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts")
   224	        target = read_text("app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts")
   225	        targets = read_text("app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts")

   235	        for rel in [
   236	            "app/api/zl/forecast/route.ts",
   237	            "app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts",
   238	            "app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts",
   239	        ]:
   240	            text = read_text(rel)

   259	
   260	    def test_boundary_overlay_attach_and_detach_paths_match_gate(self) -> None:
   261	        """[Req: inferred — chart overlay lifecycle] attach/detach should both be gated consistently."""
   262	        chart = read_text("components/chart/ZlCandlestickChart.tsx")
   263	        attach_gated = "if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {\n      series.attachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);" in chart
   264	        detach_gated = "if (SHOW_FORECAST_TARGET_OVERLAY) {\n          series.detachPrimitive(forecastTargetsPrimitive);" in chart
   265	        self.assertTrue(attach_gated)
   266	        self.assertTrue(detach_gated)
   267	
   268	    def test_boundary_pipeline_dispatch_train_passes_approved_flag(self) -> None:
   269	        """[Req: inferred — run_phase dispatch] train dispatch passes approval argument through."""
   270	        captured: dict[str, object] = {}
   271	
   272	        def fake_train(*, dry_run: bool, approved: bool) -> dict[str, object]:
   273	            captured["dry_run"] = dry_run
   274	            captured["approved"] = approved
   275	            return {"ok": True}
   276	
   277	        with patch.dict(pipeline.PHASE_MAP, {"train": fake_train}, clear=False):
   278	            pipeline.run_phase(
   279	                "train",
   280	                dry_run=True,
   281	                approve_training=True,
   282	                approve_promotion=False,
   283	            )
   284	
   285	        self.assertTrue(captured["dry_run"])
   286	        self.assertTrue(captured["approved"])
   287

   290	    unittest.main()

### BUG-001: Intraday route never executes documented 1-minute fallback
- Source: Code Review (Pass 1 + Pass 2)
- Primary requirement: REQ-001
- Severity: HIGH
- divergence_type: code-spec
- Disposition: code-fix
- fix_type: code
- Location: app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23, app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:41-46
- Spec basis: REQ-001 requires executable 15m->1m fallback and source labeling aligned to the active table.
- Expected behavior: When "'`mkt.price_15m` returns no usable rows, `GET()` queries `mkt.price_1m` and returns bars with source metadata reflecting the fallback path.
- Actual behavior: `GET()` only queries `mkt.price_15m` and always emits `source: "mkt.price_15m"`.
- Evidence: `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:17-23`, `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:45`, `supabase/migrations/202603180002_mkt.sql:18-19`.
- Covers: [REQ-001/cell-PRICE_1M-INTRADAY_GET]
- Minimal reproduction: Read `app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts`; there is no `.from("price_1m")` query path.

- Regression patch: quality/patches/BUG-001-regression-test.patch
- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-001-fix.patch
- Disposition rationale: The schema already provides `mkt.price_1m`; the divergence is implementation-only and should be fixed in route logic.
- Proposed fix: Add a second query branch to `mkt.price_1m` when the first query returns an empty/invalid row set, and set `source` from the table actually used.

### BUG-002: Forecast-targets route diverges from canonical envelope contract
- Source: Code Review (Pass 2)
- Primary requirement: REQ-002
- Severity: MEDIUM
- divergence_type: code-spec
- Disposition: code-fix
- fix_type: code
- Location: app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-85, app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106

- Expected behavior: `/api/zl/forecast-targets` and `/api/zl/target-zones` share canonical envelope keys (`ok`, `data`, `asOf`) for equivalent payload semantics.
- Actual behavior: `/api/zl/target-zones` emits `ApiEnvelope`, while `/api/zl/forecast-targets` emits `{asOfDate, targets}`.
- Evidence: `app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-85`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:59-71`, `app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106`.

- Minimal reproduction: Compare response literals in both route handlers; forecast-targets does not construct `ApiEnvelope` keys.

- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-002-fix.patch

### BUG-003: `ops.ingest_run.status` vocabulary diverges across SQL and TypeScript writers
- Source: Code Review (Pass 1 + Pass 2 + Pass 3)
- Primary requirement: REQ-003
- Severity: MEDIUM
- divergence_type: code-spec
- Disposition: code-fix
- fix_type: code
- Location: lib/server/ingest-run.ts:3-4, supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:51-52, supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:139-141, supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:56, supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:365, supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:382
- Spec basis: REQ-003 requires all `ops.ingest_run` writers to use one canonical status vocabulary.
- Expected behavior: SQL and TS producers write a single consistent set (RUNNING, SUCCESS, FAILED) to `ops.ingest_run.status`.
- Actual behavior: TS helper writes uppercase statuses while SQL jobs write lowercase/alternate values (`running`, `ok`, `failed`, `error`).
- Evidence: `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:17`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:38`, `lib/server/ingest-run.ts:58`, `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:51`, `supabase/migrations/20260414001_ingest_zl_intraday.sql:139`, `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:56`, `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:365`, `supabase/migrations/202605080003_supabase_trusted_site_fill_hourly.sql:382`.

- Consolidation rationale: All absent cells flow from one shared contract split between SQL and TS writer implementations; normalizing writer literals closes all six cells.
- Minimal reproduction: Grep writer literals in the two SQL migrations and TS helper; value sets differ.
- Regression test: quality/tests/test_bug_003_ingest_status_vocabulary.py::test_bug_003_ingest_status_vocabulary_is_single_set
- Regression patch: quality/patches/BUG-003-regression-test.patch
- Fix patch: quality/patches/BUG-003-fix.patch
- Disposition rationale: Table-level constraints do not canonicalize values; writer logic must normalize the persisted vocabulary.
- Proposed fix: Canonicalize SQL writer status literals to match TS (`RUNNING`, `SUCCESS`, `FAILED`) or enforce one enum and adapt all writers.

import re
from pathlib import Path

import pytest


ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parents[2]


@pytest.mark.xfail(strict=True, reason=\"BUG-002: remove marker after applying quality/patches/BUG-002-fix.patch\")
def test_bug_002_forecast_targets_uses_api_envelope_keys() -> None:
    source = (ROOT / \"app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts\").read_text(encoding=\"utf-8\")

    ok_key = re.search(r\"return\\\\s+NextResponse\\\\.json\\\\(\\\\{["'^}]*'"\\\\bok\\\\s*:\", source, flags=re.S)
    data_key = re.search(r\"return\\\\s+NextResponse\\\\.json\\\\(\\\\{["'^}]*'"\\\\bdata\\\\s*:\", source, flags=re.S)
    asof_key = re.search(r\"return\\\\s+NextResponse\\\\.json\\\\(\\\\{["'^}]*'"\\\\basOf\\\\s*:\", source, flags=re.S)

    assert ok_key is not None
    assert data_key is not None
    assert asof_key is not None

### Shared Concept: Fallback behavior and downstream contract assumptions
- Requirements: REQ-001, REQ-002
- What REQ-001 claims: Intraday path executes declared fallback and reports the data source used.
- What REQ-002 claims: Equivalent forecast-target APIs expose one stable envelope contract.

- Code evidence: app/api/zl/intraday/route.ts:16-23,45; app/api/zl/target-zones/route.ts:80-85; app/api/zl/forecast-targets/route.ts:103-106

- Impact: Higher client fragility and harder degraded-mode behavior verification.

- Requirements: REQ-002, REQ-005
- What REQ-002 claims: Forecast-target endpoints should expose one stable response contract.
- What REQ-005 claims: AI-first routes with runtime pulls must preserve degraded/fallback transparency.
- Consistency: CONSISTENT
- Code evidence: app/api/strategy/posture/route.ts:233-256; app/api/sentiment/overview/route.ts:188-193
- Analysis: Degraded-mode metadata is present on AI-first card routes; the known mismatch is localized to forecast-target envelope shape, not fallback metadata handling.

- Requirements: REQ-003, REQ-010, REQ-011

- What REQ-010/011 claim: Audit artifacts should be canonicalized and interpretable.
- Consistency: INCONSISTENT

- Analysis: Review/audit workflows relying on one status taxonomy can misinterpret ingest health due to writer divergence.
- Impact: Incorrect rollup health filtering and false-positive/false-negative operational alerts.

### Shared Concept: Approval gates and mechanical verification boundaries

/bin/zsh -lc "python - <<'PY'
import json,re
from pathlib import Path
bugs=Path('quality/BUGS.md').read_text()
cover_re=re.compile(r'"'^- Covers: '"\\[(.*?)\\]"'$'"',re.M)
covers=[]
for m in cover_re.finditer(bugs):
    covers.extend([x.strip() for x in m.group(1).split(',') if x.strip()])
cover_set=set(covers)
grid=json.loads(Path('quality/compensation_grid.json').read_text())
downg=json.loads(Path('quality/compensation_grid_downgrades.json').read_text())
down_set={d['cell_id'] for d in downg.get('downgrades',[])}
for req,entry in grid['reqs'].items():
    abs_set={c['cell_id'] for c in entry['cells'] if c['present'] is False}
    covered=(cover_set|down_set)
    missing=abs_set-covered
    print(req,'absent',len(abs_set),'covered',len(abs_set-missing),'missing',len(missing))
    if missing:
        print('  missing:',sorted(missing))
PY" in /Users/zincdigital/mnt/SatechiHub/ZINC-FUSION-V16
